  </div>

    {{ range $pages }}
      <article class="blog-preview">
        <h3><a href="{{ .RelPermalink }}">{{ .Title }}</a></h3>
        <p class="article-meta">{{ .Date.Format (i18n "date.format") }}</p>
        <div class="article-summary markdown-content">
          {{ .Summary | markdownify }}
        </div>

      </article>
    {{ end }}
  {{ else }}

  {{ end }}
</main>
{{ end }}

<script>
window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
  const aLaUne = document.getElementById('a-la-une');
  const header = document.querySelector('.site-header');
  if (!aLaUne || !header) return;
  const headerHeight = header.offsetHeight;
  const scrollY = window.scrollY;

  if (scrollY < 100) {
    aLaUne.classList.add('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
  } else {
    aLaUne.classList.remove('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = '';
  }
});
</script>

let modeLivraison = "domicile";

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  // Tranches de poids en grammes, tarifs en euros
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  // --- NOUVEAU : applique la s√©lection m√©moris√©e ---
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; // applique la s√©lection m√©moris√©e
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; // m√©morise la s√©lection
      afficherPanier();           // et rafra√Æchit le panier
    };
  }

  // --- Calculs ---
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}


function fermerPanier() {
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'none';
}

function validerPanier() {
  // Calculs pour affichage
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  const total = prix_total_cds + frais;
  
  // G√©n√®re un r√©sum√© simple √† recopier
  const resumeCommande = `Articles: ${panier.map(item => `${item.titre} (${item.quantite})`).join(', ')} - Livraison: ${modeLivraison === 'domicile' ? 'Domicile' : 'Point relais'} - Total: ${total.toFixed(2)} ‚Ç¨`;

  // Affiche le r√©capitulatif simple
  let panierHtml = `
    <h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre commande</h2>
    <div style="background:#e8f5e8; padding:1.5em; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em; border:2px solid #4CAF50;">
      <div style="font-size:1.1em; margin-bottom:1em;"><strong>Copiez ce texte :</strong></div>
      <div style="background:white; padding:1em; border-radius:4px; font-family:monospace; border:1px dashed #666; color:#333; font-size:1.1em;">${resumeCommande}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
      <strong>1.</strong> Copiez le texte ci-dessus (s√©lectionnez + Ctrl+C)<br>
      <strong>2.</strong> Cliquez sur le bouton ci-dessous<br>
      <strong>3.</strong> Collez votre commande dans le formulaire (Ctrl+V)
    </p>
    <a href="/contact/" style="display:block; width:100%; padding:1em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; text-decoration:none; text-align:center; border-radius:8px; font-size:1.2em; font-weight:bold;">Aller au formulaire de contact</a>
  `;
  
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
}

function closeCdPopup() {
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const modalCd = document.getElementById('cd-popup');
  if (modalCd && modalCd.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalCd) closeCdPopup();
  const modalPanier = document.getElementById('panier-popup');
  if (modalPanier && modalPanier.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalPanier) fermerPanier();
});
</script>
{{ end }}

===== ./content/jeux/_index.en.md =====

---
title: "Video Games"
---

## Video Game Creator

Passionate about interactivity and storytelling, I design video games where music, scenario and immersive experience come together.

My video games are adaptations of my original works created in interactive exhibitions in reality. A new medium where the listener is active!

My purpose is to make the approach to contemporary music, particularly acousmatic, playful through direct interaction.

<div><br><br>

---

</div>

## My Games

All my games are bilingual French | English and available for Linux and Windows.

Headphones or a 5.1 surround system is recommended.

Pour le jeu, j'ai gard√© cette id√©e : le joueur explore un univers musical, mais au lieu de sculptures, il clique sur des √©l√©ments visuels qui d√©clenchent des s√©quences sonores. ===== ./content/blog/interview-arthur-gyl-jean-christophe.en.md =====

---
title: "Arthur Gyl interviews Jean-Christophe Ploquin"
date: 2025-06-07
draft: false
summary: "**Arthur Gyl** and **Jean-Christophe Ploquin** discuss the creation of interactive musical games. How to transition from the *Music & Me* exhibition to video games? A fascinating conversation about artistic innovation and technical challenges."
---

## Arthur Gyl interviews Jean-Christophe Ploquin

**Arthur Gyl:** So Jean-Christophe, here we are again! This time, I'd like to understand how you create your musical games. Where does this strange idea of mixing music and gameplay come from?

**Jean-Christophe Ploquin:** *[laughs]* Strange, you say? Coming from someone who writes science fiction, that's rich! But seriously, it all started with the acousmatic-plastic exhibition *"Music & Me"* that I created with Louis Jeanne in 2022. The audience really appreciated discovering acousmatic music in a playful and interactive way. Then my son Alexandre finished his animation studies at Lanim√©a and started designing a point-and-click game. That gave me an idea! What if I adapted *"Music & Me"* into a video game?

**A.G.:** Ah, family influence! But concretely, how do you go from an exhibition with sound sculptures to a video game? It's not the same medium at all!

**J-C.P.:** Exactly! That's where it gets exciting. In the exhibition, visitors touched sculptures to trigger sounds, created their own compositions... The principle was already interactive. For the game, I kept this idea: the player explores a musical universe, but instead of sculptures, they click on visual elements that trigger sound sequences. The music builds up as exploration progresses.

**A.G.:** Wait, you're telling me that the music changes according to what the player does? How do you do that technically? Because when I write, my words don't change depending on who reads them!

**J-C.P.:** *[laughs]* Ah, but imagine if your novels adapted to the reader! Actually, I use "stems" - separate musical layers that I can activate or deactivate in real time. With Godot as the game engine and Ardour for audio, I create musical loops that assemble differently according to the player's actions. It's like having a virtual orchestra that reacts to clicks!

**A.G.:** Godot, Ardour... you're speaking Chinese! But tell me, what was your biggest failure? There must have been moments when it turned into total cacophony?

**J-C.P.:** Oh my! *[laughs]* I remember a bug where all the tracks triggered at the same time instead of alternating. Imagine 15 different musical loops superimposing all at once! It was... let's say... very experimental! But sometimes, these accidents give ideas. That bug inspired me to create a sequence where musical chaos is part of the gameplay.

**A.G.:** But concretely, what do you start with? The music or the gameplay?

**J-C.P.:** The music, of course! The gameplay is just the interactive layer that allows the listener to act on the music. All musical possibilities must be considered beforehand, and validated as musically interesting. It's non-linear writing, composition by reservoirs, where nothing is really left to chance.

**A.G.:** What's the biggest challenge? Making music or making a game?

**J-C.P.:** They're completely different: both are enormous challenges, each in their own way, but music depends on my creativity while the game depends on my technical skills.

**A.G.:** Do you want to educate people about acousmatic music or just entertain them?

**J-C.P.:** Thirty years in the national education system and I would continue teaching? No, seriously, I seek to entertain them above all. We say "play music": it's a game! We must have fun! If they learn things at the same time, well, so much the better.

**A.G.:** And now, you're working on Ascendance... What's the difference?

**J-C.P.:** "Ascendance" is the adaptation of a play that I never had the pleasure of having performed; a game based on genealogy, another of my obsessions. A tragicomic journey to meet ancestors, also built on non-linear reservoirs. Any family tree can be loaded into the game: the journeys are different each time. But I'm not working on it anymore: it's finished and comes out on June 9th. I'm already on another project.

**A.G.:** But you never stop! It's bulimia! And what will it be this time?

**J-C.P.:** "GraviTone", an adaptation of the video-musical exhibition "Fluctus Planetarium"; another of my projects with Louis Jeanne.

**A.G.:** And then you stop!

**J-C.P.:** Never!

**A.G.:** You'll still have to let me write from time to time... People are asking for the sequel to the homo permanens adventures!

**J-C.P.:** Promise. I'll leave you a slot.

title: "Home"

## Hydrophonia

My latest symphonic poem created for the Nautil'Art 2023 Festival at the Halle aux Toiles in Rouen.

This 60-minute composition explores the aquatic element through four cyclical movements with no defined beginning or end.

**I. Aquastasis** - The primordial aquatic balance  
**II. Cosmogenesis** - The cosmic birth of waters  
**III. Exolvuntur** - The evolution of aquatic forms  
**IV. Fons Vitae** - The universal source of life

## Interactive creations

Discover my musical games on itch.io, where music becomes interactive and immersive. A transmedia approach that unites electroacoustic composition and digital interactivity.

title: "Literature"

## Arthur Gyl: my other self

Passionate about imagination and future worlds, I explore in my novels and short stories the boundaries between science, humanity and destiny. My universe revolves around the "From Death to Life" cycle, where adventure, reflection and poetry intertwine.

<div><br><br>

---

<br></div>

### The "From Death to Life" cycle

What if the boundary between death and life became a stage in a larger cycle?

Immersed in a future where science meets destiny, this cycle explores the fate of ordinary beings confronted with the extraordinary: life after death, absolute memory, the games of power and infinity...

Through several generations and worlds, each volume weaves a fresco where adventure, reflection and poetry intertwine, questioning what makes us human... and what transcends us.

A science fiction saga where each answer raises new questions, and where the journey matters as much as the destination, each volume revealing a new facet of the same mystery...

## Hydrophonia

Mon dernier po√®me symphonique cr√©√© pour le Festival Nautil'Art 2023 √† la Halle aux Toiles de Rouen.

Cette composition de 60 minutes explore l'√©l√©ment aquatique √† travers quatre mouvements cycliques sans d√©but ni fin d√©finie.

**I. Aquastasis** - L'√©quilibre aquatique primordial  
**II. Cosmogenesis** - La naissance cosmique des eaux  
**III. Exolvuntur** - L'√©volution des formes aquatiques  
**IV. Fons Vitae** - La source de vie universelle

## Cr√©ations interactives

===== ./content/about/_index.en.md =====

---
title: "About Me"
---
<img src="/img/JCPloquin.jpg" alt="Hydrophonia Portrait" style="max-width:320px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:2rem auto;">

## Biography

Electroacoustic composer and guitarist, I am passionate about musical creation in all its forms: from fingerpicking blues and Celtic music to acousmatic music, including contemporary composition and interactive installations.

After studying musicology and winning first prize in electroacoustics at the Dieppe conservatory, I explored the live scene, radio creation on Second Life, Celtic music with Normainn, then science fiction writing.

My artistic universe, nourished by family tradition and technological innovation, oscillates between transmission, experimentation and sound immersion.

---

## An exceptional musical heritage

Music has been flowing in my veins for several generations. Besides my grandfather and my father, both passionate pianists, my family also includes prominent figures from the French musical scene.

<div style="display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 100px; align-items: flex-end;">
  <div>
    <img src="/img/CharlesPloquin.png" alt="My grandfather" style="max-width:120px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:auto;">
    <div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.8em;">Charles Ploquin, 1930s</div>
  </div>
  <div>
    <img src="/img/JeanPloquin.png" alt="My father" style="max-width:120px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:auto;">
    <div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.8em;">Jean Ploquin, 1950s</div>
  </div>
</div>

Among them, **Mathurin Fran√ßois Furic**, better known as **Matilin an Dall** ("Mathurin the blind"), is undoubtedly the most legendary. Born in Quimperl√© in 1789, becoming blind at a very young age, he established himself as one of the greatest bombard players in Brittany. A true virtuoso, he played at all the great Breton festivals, but also before political personalities and even before Napoleon III during his visit to Quimper in 1858.

> *"Celtic Paganini, king of the gavotte, genius of the Breton oboe... Matilin an Dall marked his era and left an indelible mark on traditional music."*  
> ‚Äî Pierre Larousse, Grand Universal Dictionary of the 19th Century

He inspired many writers and musicians, and his name remains associated with excellence and Breton musical tradition.

<img src="/img/Matilin-an-dall.jpg" alt="Mathurin Furic" style="max-width:200px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:2rem auto;">

[Learn more about Matilin an Dall (Wikipedia)](https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matilin_an_Dall)

---

### Marthe Ploquin, committed artist

<img src="/img/MarthePloquin.jpg" alt="Marthe Ploquin" style="max-width:200px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:2rem auto;">

My great-great-aunt, Marthe Ploquin, was also a recognized figure in the La Rochelle musical world, both as a pianist and as a singer, famous for her charity concerts for the benefit of Great War soldiers. Her commitment and talent are still praised today, as evidenced by a recent article from the Departmental Archives of Charente-Maritime:

[Read the complete article on Marthe Ploquin, a musician in the Great War](https://archives.charente-maritime.fr/actualites/doc-du-mois-marthe-ploquin-une-musicienne-dans-grande-guerre)

The local press was full of praise for her performances:

> *"Miss Ploquin made us admire her remarkable technique. She easily handled the double-note passages of the Andante and brilliantly performed the Allegro and Presto. An intelligent interpreter, Miss Ploquin dazzled us with her virtuosity."*  
> ‚Äî Le Courrier de La Rochelle, December 13, 1919

---

**This family heritage, made of passion, transmission and commitment, continues to inspire my own artistic journey.**

});

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; 
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; 
      afficherPanier();           
    };
  }

  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}


function fermerPanier() {
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'none';
}

function validerPanier() {
  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  const total = prix_total_cds + frais;
  
  
  const resumeCommande = `Articles: ${panier.map(item => `${item.titre} (${item.quantite})`).join(', ')} - Livraison: ${modeLivraison === 'domicile' ? 'Domicile' : 'Point relais'} - Total: ${total.toFixed(2)} ‚Ç¨`;

  
  let panierHtml = `
    <h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre commande</h2>
    <div style="background:#e8f5e8; padding:1.5em; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em; border:2px solid #4CAF50;">
      <div style="font-size:1.1em; margin-bottom:1em;"><strong>Copiez ce texte :</strong></div>
      <div style="background:white; padding:1em; border-radius:4px; font-family:monospace; border:1px dashed #666; color:#333; font-size:1.1em;">${resumeCommande}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
      <strong>1.</strong> Copiez le texte ci-dessus (s√©lectionnez + Ctrl+C)<br>
      <strong>2.</strong> Cliquez sur le bouton ci-dessous<br>
      <strong>3.</strong> Collez votre commande dans le formulaire (Ctrl+V)
    </p>
    <a href="/contact/" style="display:block; width:100%; padding:1em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; text-decoration:none; text-align:center; border-radius:8px; font-size:1.2em; font-weight:bold;">Aller au formulaire de contact</a>
  `;
  
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
}

function closeCdPopup() {
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const modalCd = document.getElementById('cd-popup');
  if (modalCd && modalCd.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalCd) closeCdPopup();
  const modalPanier = document.getElementById('panier-popup');
  if (modalPanier && modalPanier.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalPanier) fermerPanier();
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

<article class="single-page">
    <div class="container">
        <header class="page-header">
            <h1>Arthur Gyl interviews Jean-Christophe Ploquin</h1>
            <p class="article-meta">June 7, 2025</p>
        </header>
        <div class="page-content markdown-content">
            <h2 id="arthur-gyl-interviews-jean-christophe-ploquin">Arthur Gyl interviews Jean-Christophe Ploquin</h2>
<p><strong>Arthur Gyl:</strong> So Jean-Christophe, here we are again! This time, I&rsquo;d like to understand how you create your musical games. Where does this strange idea of mixing music and gameplay come from?</p>
<p><strong>Jean-Christophe Ploquin:</strong> <em>[laughs]</em> Strange, you say? Coming from someone who writes science fiction, that&rsquo;s rich! But seriously, it all started with the acousmatic-plastic exhibition <em>&ldquo;Music &amp; Me&rdquo;</em> that I created with Louis Jeanne in 2022. The audience really appreciated discovering acousmatic music in a playful and interactive way. Then my son Alexandre finished his animation studies at Lanim√©a and started designing a point-and-click game. That gave me an idea! What if I adapted <em>&ldquo;Music &amp; Me&rdquo;</em> into a video game?</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> Ah, family influence! But concretely, how do you go from an exhibition with sound sculptures to a video game? It&rsquo;s not the same medium at all!</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> Exactly! That&rsquo;s where it gets exciting. In the exhibition, visitors touched sculptures to trigger sounds, created their own compositions&hellip; The principle was already interactive. For the game, I kept this idea: the player explores a musical universe, but instead of sculptures, they click on visual elements that trigger sound sequences. The music builds up as exploration progresses.</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> Wait, you&rsquo;re telling me that the music changes according to what the player does? How do you do that technically? Because when I write, my words don&rsquo;t change depending on who reads them!</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> <em>[laughs]</em> Ah, but imagine if your novels adapted to the reader! Actually, I use &ldquo;stems&rdquo; - separate musical layers that I can activate or deactivate in real time. With Godot as the game engine and Ardour for audio, I create musical loops that assemble differently according to the player&rsquo;s actions. It&rsquo;s like having a virtual orchestra that reacts to clicks!</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> Godot, Ardour&hellip; you&rsquo;re speaking Chinese! But tell me, what was your biggest failure? There must have been moments when it turned into total cacophony?</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> Oh my! <em>[laughs]</em> I remember a bug where all the tracks triggered at the same time instead of alternating. Imagine 15 different musical loops superimposing all at once! It was&hellip; let&rsquo;s say&hellip; very experimental! But sometimes, these accidents give ideas. That bug inspired me to create a sequence where musical chaos is part of the gameplay.</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> But concretely, what do you start with? The music or the gameplay?</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> The music, of course! The gameplay is just the interactive layer that allows the listener to act on the music. All musical possibilities must be considered beforehand, and validated as musically interesting. It&rsquo;s non-linear writing, composition by reservoirs, where nothing is really left to chance.</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> What&rsquo;s the biggest challenge? Making music or making a game?</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> They&rsquo;re completely different: both are enormous challenges, each in their own way, but music depends on my creativity while the game depends on my technical skills.</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> Do you want to educate people about acousmatic music or just entertain them?</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> Thirty years in the national education system and I would continue teaching? No, seriously, I seek to entertain them above all. We say &ldquo;play music&rdquo;: it&rsquo;s a game! We must have fun! If they learn things at the same time, well, so much the better.</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> And now, you&rsquo;re working on Ascendance&hellip; What&rsquo;s the difference?</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> &ldquo;Ascendance&rdquo; is the adaptation of a play that I never had the pleasure of having performed; a game based on genealogy, another of my obsessions. A tragicomic journey to meet ancestors, also built on non-linear reservoirs. Any family tree can be loaded into the game: the journeys are different each time. But I&rsquo;m not working on it anymore: it&rsquo;s finished and comes out on June 9th. I&rsquo;m already on another project.</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> But you never stop! It&rsquo;s bulimia! And what will it be this time?</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> &ldquo;GraviTone&rdquo;, an adaptation of the video-musical exhibition &ldquo;Fluctus Planetarium&rdquo;; another of my projects with Louis Jeanne.</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> And then you stop!</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> Never!</p>
<p><strong>A.G.:</strong> You&rsquo;ll still have to let me write from time to time&hellip; People are asking for the sequel to the homo permanens adventures!</p>
<p><strong>J-C.P.:</strong> Promise. I&rsquo;ll leave you a slot.</p>

        </div>
        
        
        
    </div>
</article>

        <p>Haptic music and immersive installations - Science fiction novels</p>

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; 
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; 
      afficherPanier();           
    };
  }

  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}


function fermerPanier() {
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'none';
}

function validerPanier() {
  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  const total = prix_total_cds + frais;
  
  
  const resumeCommande = `Articles: ${panier.map(item => `${item.titre} (${item.quantite})`).join(', ')} - Livraison: ${modeLivraison === 'domicile' ? 'Domicile' : 'Point relais'} - Total: ${total.toFixed(2)} ‚Ç¨`;

  
  let panierHtml = `
    <h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre commande</h2>
    <div style="background:#e8f5e8; padding:1.5em; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em; border:2px solid #4CAF50;">
      <div style="font-size:1.1em; margin-bottom:1em;"><strong>Copiez ce texte :</strong></div>
      <div style="background:white; padding:1em; border-radius:4px; font-family:monospace; border:1px dashed #666; color:#333; font-size:1.1em;">${resumeCommande}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
      <strong>1.</strong> Copiez le texte ci-dessus (s√©lectionnez + Ctrl+C)<br>
      <strong>2.</strong> Cliquez sur le bouton ci-dessous<br>
      <strong>3.</strong> Collez votre commande dans le formulaire (Ctrl+V)
    </p>
    <a href="/contact/" style="display:block; width:100%; padding:1em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; text-decoration:none; text-align:center; border-radius:8px; font-size:1.2em; font-weight:bold;">Aller au formulaire de contact</a>
  `;
  
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
}

function closeCdPopup() {
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const modalCd = document.getElementById('cd-popup');
  if (modalCd && modalCd.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalCd) closeCdPopup();
  const modalPanier = document.getElementById('panier-popup');
  if (modalPanier && modalPanier.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalPanier) fermerPanier();
});
</script>

</body>

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; 
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; 
      afficherPanier();           
    };
  }

  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}

let modeLivraison = "domicile";

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; 
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; 
      afficherPanier();           
    };
  }

  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}


function fermerPanier() {
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'none';
}

function validerPanier() {
  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  const total = prix_total_cds + frais;
  
  
  const resumeCommande = `Articles: ${panier.map(item => `${item.titre} (${item.quantite})`).join(', ')} - Livraison: ${modeLivraison === 'domicile' ? 'Domicile' : 'Point relais'} - Total: ${total.toFixed(2)} ‚Ç¨`;

  
  let panierHtml = `
    <h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre commande</h2>
    <div style="background:#e8f5e8; padding:1.5em; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em; border:2px solid #4CAF50;">
      <div style="font-size:1.1em; margin-bottom:1em;"><strong>Copiez ce texte :</strong></div>
      <div style="background:white; padding:1em; border-radius:4px; font-family:monospace; border:1px dashed #666; color:#333; font-size:1.1em;">${resumeCommande}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
      <strong>1.</strong> Copiez le texte ci-dessus (s√©lectionnez + Ctrl+C)<br>
      <strong>2.</strong> Cliquez sur le bouton ci-dessous<br>
      <strong>3.</strong> Collez votre commande dans le formulaire (Ctrl+V)
    </p>
    <a href="/contact/" style="display:block; width:100%; padding:1em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; text-decoration:none; text-align:center; border-radius:8px; font-size:1.2em; font-weight:bold;">Aller au formulaire de contact</a>
  `;
  
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
}

function closeCdPopup() {
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const modalCd = document.getElementById('cd-popup');
  if (modalCd && modalCd.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalCd) closeCdPopup();
  const modalPanier = document.getElementById('panier-popup');
  if (modalPanier && modalPanier.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalPanier) fermerPanier();
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

  const aLaUne = document.getElementById('a-la-une');
  const header = document.querySelector('.site-header');
  if (!aLaUne || !header) return;
  const headerHeight = header.offsetHeight;
  const scrollY = window.scrollY;

  if (scrollY < 100) {
    aLaUne.classList.add('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
  } else {
    aLaUne.classList.remove('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = '';
  }
});

<main class="content-section">
  <h1>Literature</h1>
  <div>
    <h2 id="arthur-gyl-my-other-self">Arthur Gyl: my other self</h2>
<p>Passionate about imagination and future worlds, I explore in my novels and short stories the boundaries between science, humanity and destiny. My universe revolves around the &ldquo;From Death to Life&rdquo; cycle, where adventure, reflection and poetry intertwine.</p>
<div><br><br>
<hr>
<p><br></div></p>
<h3 id="the-from-death-to-life-cycle">The &ldquo;From Death to Life&rdquo; cycle</h3>
<p>What if the boundary between death and life became a stage in a larger cycle?</p>
<p>Immersed in a future where science meets destiny, this cycle explores the fate of ordinary beings confronted with the extraordinary: life after death, absolute memory, the games of power and infinity&hellip;</p>
<p>Through several generations and worlds, each volume weaves a fresco where adventure, reflection and poetry intertwine, questioning what makes us human&hellip; and what transcends us.</p>
<p>A science fiction saga where each answer raises new questions, and where the journey matters as much as the destination, each volume revealing a new facet of the same mystery&hellip;</p>
<h3 id="excerpts">Excerpts</h3>

function openModal(url) {
  document.getElementById('flipbook-frame').src = url;
  document.getElementById('flipbook-modal').style.display = 'flex';
}
function closeModal() {
  document.getElementById('flipbook-modal').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('flipbook-frame').src = '';
}

  var modal = document.getElementById('flipbook-modal');
  if (modal.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modal) closeModal();
});

let modeLivraison = "domicile";

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; 
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; 
      afficherPanier();           
    };
  }

  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}


function fermerPanier() {
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'none';
}

function validerPanier() {
  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  const total = prix_total_cds + frais;
  
  
  const resumeCommande = `Articles: ${panier.map(item => `${item.titre} (${item.quantite})`).join(', ')} - Livraison: ${modeLivraison === 'domicile' ? 'Domicile' : 'Point relais'} - Total: ${total.toFixed(2)} ‚Ç¨`;

  
  let panierHtml = `
    <h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre commande</h2>
    <div style="background:#e8f5e8; padding:1.5em; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em; border:2px solid #4CAF50;">
      <div style="font-size:1.1em; margin-bottom:1em;"><strong>Copiez ce texte :</strong></div>
      <div style="background:white; padding:1em; border-radius:4px; font-family:monospace; border:1px dashed #666; color:#333; font-size:1.1em;">${resumeCommande}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
      <strong>1.</strong> Copiez le texte ci-dessus (s√©lectionnez + Ctrl+C)<br>
      <strong>2.</strong> Cliquez sur le bouton ci-dessous<br>
      <strong>3.</strong> Collez votre commande dans le formulaire (Ctrl+V)
    </p>
    <a href="/contact/" style="display:block; width:100%; padding:1em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; text-decoration:none; text-align:center; border-radius:8px; font-size:1.2em; font-weight:bold;">Aller au formulaire de contact</a>
  `;
  
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
}

function closeCdPopup() {
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const modalCd = document.getElementById('cd-popup');
  if (modalCd && modalCd.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalCd) closeCdPopup();
  const modalPanier = document.getElementById('panier-popup');
  if (modalPanier && modalPanier.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalPanier) fermerPanier();
});
</script>

window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
  const aLaUne = document.getElementById('a-la-une');
  const header = document.querySelector('.site-header');
  if (!aLaUne || !header) return;
  const headerHeight = header.offsetHeight;
  const scrollY = window.scrollY;

  if (scrollY < 100) {
    aLaUne.classList.add('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
  } else {
    aLaUne.classList.remove('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = '';
  }
});
</script>

<main class="content-section">
  <h1>About Me</h1>
  <div>
    <img src="/img/JCPloquin.jpg" alt="Hydrophonia Portrait" style="max-width:320px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:2rem auto;">
<h2 id="biography">Biography</h2>
<p>Electroacoustic composer and guitarist, I am passionate about musical creation in all its forms: from fingerpicking blues and Celtic music to acousmatic music, including contemporary composition and interactive installations.</p>
<p>After studying musicology and winning first prize in electroacoustics at the Dieppe conservatory, I explored the live scene, radio creation on Second Life, Celtic music with Normainn, then science fiction writing.</p>
<p>My artistic universe, nourished by family tradition and technological innovation, oscillates between transmission, experimentation and sound immersion.</p>
<hr>
<h2 id="an-exceptional-musical-heritage">An exceptional musical heritage</h2>
<p>Music has been flowing in my veins for several generations. Besides my grandfather and my father, both passionate pianists, my family also includes prominent figures from the French musical scene.</p>
<div style="display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 100px; align-items: flex-end;">
  <div>
    <img src="/img/CharlesPloquin.png" alt="My grandfather" style="max-width:120px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:auto;">
    <div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.8em;">Charles Ploquin, 1930s</div>
  </div>
  <div>
    <img src="/img/JeanPloquin.png" alt="My father" style="max-width:120px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:auto;">
    <div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.8em;">Jean Ploquin, 1950s</div>
  </div>
</div>
<p>Among them, <strong>Mathurin Fran√ßois Furic</strong>, better known as <strong>Matilin an Dall</strong> (&ldquo;Mathurin the blind&rdquo;), is undoubtedly the most legendary. Born in Quimperl√© in 1789, becoming blind at a very young age, he established himself as one of the greatest bombard players in Brittany. A true virtuoso, he played at all the great Breton festivals, but also before political personalities and even before Napoleon III during his visit to Quimper in 1858.</p>
<blockquote>
<p><em>&ldquo;Celtic Paganini, king of the gavotte, genius of the Breton oboe&hellip; Matilin an Dall marked his era and left an indelible mark on traditional music.&quot;</em><br>
‚Äî Pierre Larousse, Grand Universal Dictionary of the 19th Century</p>
</blockquote>
<p>He inspired many writers and musicians, and his name remains associated with excellence and Breton musical tradition.</p>
<img src="/img/Matilin-an-dall.jpg" alt="Mathurin Furic" style="max-width:200px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:2rem auto;">
<p><a href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matilin_an_Dall">Learn more about Matilin an Dall (Wikipedia)</a></p>
<hr>
<h3 id="marthe-ploquin-committed-artist">Marthe Ploquin, committed artist</h3>
<img src="/img/MarthePloquin.jpg" alt="Marthe Ploquin" style="max-width:200px; width:100%; height:auto; display:block; margin:2rem auto;">
<p>My great-great-aunt, Marthe Ploquin, was also a recognized figure in the La Rochelle musical world, both as a pianist and as a singer, famous for her charity concerts for the benefit of Great War soldiers. Her commitment and talent are still praised today, as evidenced by a recent article from the Departmental Archives of Charente-Maritime:</p>
<p><a href="https://archives.charente-maritime.fr/actualites/doc-du-mois-marthe-ploquin-une-musicienne-dans-grande-guerre">Read the complete article on Marthe Ploquin, a musician in the Great War</a></p>
<p>The local press was full of praise for her performances:</p>
<blockquote>
<p><em>&ldquo;Miss Ploquin made us admire her remarkable technique. She easily handled the double-note passages of the Andante and brilliantly performed the Allegro and Presto. An intelligent interpreter, Miss Ploquin dazzled us with her virtuosity.&quot;</em><br>
‚Äî Le Courrier de La Rochelle, December 13, 1919</p>
</blockquote>
<hr>
<p><strong>This family heritage, made of passion, transmission and commitment, continues to inspire my own artistic journey.</strong></p>

  </div>

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; 
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; 
      afficherPanier();           
    };
  }

  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}


function fermerPanier() {
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'none';
}

function validerPanier() {
  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  const total = prix_total_cds + frais;
  
  
  const resumeCommande = `Articles: ${panier.map(item => `${item.titre} (${item.quantite})`).join(', ')} - Livraison: ${modeLivraison === 'domicile' ? 'Domicile' : 'Point relais'} - Total: ${total.toFixed(2)} ‚Ç¨`;

  
  let panierHtml = `
    <h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre commande</h2>
    <div style="background:#e8f5e8; padding:1.5em; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em; border:2px solid #4CAF50;">
      <div style="font-size:1.1em; margin-bottom:1em;"><strong>Copiez ce texte :</strong></div>
      <div style="background:white; padding:1em; border-radius:4px; font-family:monospace; border:1px dashed #666; color:#333; font-size:1.1em;">${resumeCommande}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
      <strong>1.</strong> Copiez le texte ci-dessus (s√©lectionnez + Ctrl+C)<br>
      <strong>2.</strong> Cliquez sur le bouton ci-dessous<br>
      <strong>3.</strong> Collez votre commande dans le formulaire (Ctrl+V)
    </p>
    <a href="/contact/" style="display:block; width:100%; padding:1em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; text-decoration:none; text-align:center; border-radius:8px; font-size:1.2em; font-weight:bold;">Aller au formulaire de contact</a>
  `;
  
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
}

function closeCdPopup() {
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const modalCd = document.getElementById('cd-popup');
  if (modalCd && modalCd.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalCd) closeCdPopup();
  const modalPanier = document.getElementById('panier-popup');
  if (modalPanier && modalPanier.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalPanier) fermerPanier();
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

let modeLivraison = "domicile";

function openCdPopup(id) {
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  let extraitsHtml = cd.extraits.map(e =>
    `<div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>${e.titre} :</strong><br>
      <audio controls src="${e.fichier}" style="width:100%; height:30px; max-width:400px; margin:0 auto;"></audio></div>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = `
    <img src="${cd.image}" alt="${cd.titre}" style="width:100%; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em;">
    <h2>${cd.titre}</h2>
    <div style="margin:0.5em 0;"><strong>Prix :</strong> ${cd.prix}</div>
    ${extraitsHtml}
    <button onclick="ajouterAuPanier('${id}')" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; border:none; border-radius:4px; cursor:pointer; margin-top:1em;">
      Ajouter au panier
    </button>
  `;
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'flex';
}
function ajouterAuPanier(id) {
	console.log("ajouterAuPanier appel√©e avec id =", id);
  const cd = cdPopups[id];
  if (!cd) return;
  const index = panier.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
  if (index >= 0) {
    panier[index].quantite++;
  } else {
    panier.push({ id, titre: cd.titre, image: cd.image, prix: cd.prix, poids: cd.poids, quantite: 1 });
  }
  // Notification visuelle
  alert(`"${cd.titre}" a √©t√© ajout√© au panier !`);
  document.getElementById('panier-btn').innerText = `üõí (${panier.length})`;
  closeCdPopup();
}
function calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison) {
  
  const tarifs = {
    domicile: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 5.25 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 7.35 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 8.65 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 9.40 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.70 },
      { poids: 5000, prix: 16.60 }
    ],
    relais: [
      { poids: 250, prix: 4.55 },
      { poids: 500, prix: 6.65 },
      { poids: 750, prix: 7.95 },
      { poids: 1000, prix: 8.70 },
      { poids: 2000, prix: 10.00 }
    ]
  };
  const grille = tarifs[modeLivraison];
  let frais = grille.find(t => poidsTotal <= t.poids)?.prix || grille[grille.length - 1].prix;
  return frais;
}

function afficherPanier() {
  let panierHtml = '<h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre panier</h2>';
  if (panier.length === 0) {
    panierHtml += '<p>Votre panier est vide.</p>';
  } else {
		panierHtml += panier.map((item, idx) => `
		  <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
			 <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.titre}" style="width:60px; height:60px; object-fit:cover; border-radius:8px; margin-right:1em;">
			 <div>
				<strong>${item.titre}</strong><br>
				<span>${item.prix} √ó 
				  <select data-idx="${idx}" class="qte-cd" style="width:3em; margin:0 0.5em;">
				    ${[...Array(10).keys()].map(n => `<option value="${n+1}"${item.quantite===n+1?' selected':''}>${n+1}</option>`).join('')}
				  </select>
				</span>
			 </div>
		  </div>
		`).join('');
  }
  panierHtml += `
    <div style="margin-top:1em;">
      <label for="livraison">Mode de livraison‚ÄØ:</label>
      <select id="livraison" style="width:100%; padding:0.5em; margin:0.5em 0;">
        <option value="domicile">Livraison √† domicile</option>
        <option value="relais">Point relais</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Frais de port‚ÄØ: <span id="frais-port"></span>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:0.5em; font-weight:bold;">
      Total √† r√©gler‚ÄØ: <span id="total"></span>
    </div>
  `;
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'flex';
  // Ajoute le listener sur tous les selects de quantit√©
	document.querySelectorAll('.qte-cd').forEach(sel => {
	  sel.addEventListener('change', function() {
		 const idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
		 panier[idx].quantite = parseInt(this.value, 10);
		 afficherPanier();
  });
});


  
  const selectLivraison = document.getElementById('livraison');
  if (selectLivraison) {
    selectLivraison.value = modeLivraison; 
    selectLivraison.onchange = function() {
      modeLivraison = this.value; 
      afficherPanier();           
    };
  }

  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  document.getElementById('frais-port').textContent = frais + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
  document.getElementById('total').textContent = (prix_total_cds + frais).toFixed(2) + '‚ÄØ‚Ç¨';
}


function fermerPanier() {
  document.getElementById('panier-popup').style.display = 'none';
}

function validerPanier() {
  
  const poidsTotal = panier.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.poids * item.quantite), 0);
  const frais = calculerFraisDePort(poidsTotal, modeLivraison);
  const prix_total_cds = panier.reduce((total, item) => {
    return total + (parseFloat(item.prix.replace('‚Ç¨','').replace(',','.')) * item.quantite);
  }, 0);
  const total = prix_total_cds + frais;
  
  
  const resumeCommande = `Articles: ${panier.map(item => `${item.titre} (${item.quantite})`).join(', ')} - Livraison: ${modeLivraison === 'domicile' ? 'Domicile' : 'Point relais'} - Total: ${total.toFixed(2)} ‚Ç¨`;

  
  let panierHtml = `
    <h2 style="margin-bottom:1em;">Votre commande</h2>
    <div style="background:#e8f5e8; padding:1.5em; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:1em; border:2px solid #4CAF50;">
      <div style="font-size:1.1em; margin-bottom:1em;"><strong>Copiez ce texte :</strong></div>
      <div style="background:white; padding:1em; border-radius:4px; font-family:monospace; border:1px dashed #666; color:#333; font-size:1.1em;">${resumeCommande}</div>
    </div>
    <p style="text-align:center; margin-bottom:1em;">
      <strong>1.</strong> Copiez le texte ci-dessus (s√©lectionnez + Ctrl+C)<br>
      <strong>2.</strong> Cliquez sur le bouton ci-dessous<br>
      <strong>3.</strong> Collez votre commande dans le formulaire (Ctrl+V)
    </p>
    <a href="/contact/" style="display:block; width:100%; padding:1em; background:#4CAF50; color:#fff; text-decoration:none; text-align:center; border-radius:8px; font-size:1.2em; font-weight:bold;">Aller au formulaire de contact</a>
  `;
  
  document.getElementById('panier-content').innerHTML = panierHtml;
}

function closeCdPopup() {
  document.getElementById('cd-popup').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('cd-popup-content').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const modalCd = document.getElementById('cd-popup');
  if (modalCd && modalCd.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalCd) closeCdPopup();
  const modalPanier = document.getElementById('panier-popup');
  if (modalPanier && modalPanier.style.display === 'flex' && e.target === modalPanier) fermerPanier();
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

<script>
window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
  const aLaUne = document.getElementById('a-la-une');
  const header = document.querySelector('.site-header');
  if (!aLaUne || !header) return;
  const headerHeight = header.offsetHeight;
  const scrollY = window.scrollY;

  if (scrollY < 100) {
    aLaUne.classList.add('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
  } else {
    aLaUne.classList.remove('floating');
    aLaUne.style.top = '';
  }
});
</script>
